hereafter folowith boke callyd myrroure oure lady necessary relygyous persones fyrste prologue ¶here begynneth prologue thys presente boke folowynge called oure ladyes myroure viderunt eam filie syon et beatissimam predicauerunt cantice vi wordes writen holy scrypture thus say englyshe doughtres syon haue sene hyr say oure lady haue shewed hyr mooste blessyd whiche wordes holy goste sayth thre haue shewed hyr mooste blessed therfore sayeth doughtres syon haue sene hyr haue shewed hyr moste blessed ¶fyrste holy goste tellyth prayse lady callyth doughtres syon though chrysten soulles treuly charite goodnes dothe ye oughte beholde also shortnes vnstablenes thys lyfe hastynes dethe ferefulnes dome bytternes paynes swyete ioyfull rewardes blysse ye thus good doughtres syon meke obedyence trew beholdynge thynges ar ye well dysposed worthyly prayse oure moste gloryous lady ¶the seconde thynge holy goste tellyth wordes y ye ought doo ye begynne prayse oure lady y ye oughte se ye wote well man ne may well shewe worthynes propertyes thynge praysynge therof yf haue fyrste som syght knowlege thinge one meane shall ye condewly shewe outwarde praysyng excellent hyghnes worthynes moste blyssed heuenly quene oure reuerente lady yt full fayre expressed al youre holy seruyce yf ye haue fyrste syght therof inwarde vnderstandinge ¶but asmoche many thoughe ye synge rede yet ye se meanynge therof y therefore onely worshyp praysyng oure lorde iesu chryste hys moste mercyfull mother oure lady gostly cōforte profyte youre soules haue drawen youre legende youre seruyce enlyshe ye shulde se vnderstōdyng therof worthy holy praysynge oure gloryous lady contente therin deuoutely knowyngly synge yt rede yt say yt worshyp ¶and many place nakyd letter thoughe yt set enlyshe y easy symple soulles vnderstonde▪ expounde yt declare yt openly letter else fourthe wyth gyther ¶and farthermore ye shulde haue sprytuall loue inwarde delyte deuocyon thys holy seruyce tell cause meanynges eche parte therof say whan come fyrste inuitory▪ tell inuitatory y say yt y namyd set suche place psalmes hympnes antempnes respōces versicle suche declare ar callyd y say hympne y callyd hympne antepmne capitulo xi ¶and hereof ye haue notable example saynt maudes reuelaciōs bothe diuine seruyce howslyng lyke man agenst lordes comyng hym maketh clene house yf may hast cast ye vnclēnesse entrey thē swepeth yt vp togyther corner castyth yt oute afterwarde ryghte whan persone goyth dyuyne seruyce howslynge felyth grudgeyng cōscyence yf may get gostly father shryue hym ought sorowe hys synnes harte contricion shryue therof god swepe yt corner hys mynde tyll may gette hys confessour trustynge oure lordes mercy go hys seruice hys howslyng ¶this kepte time synnes dyuyne seruyce also kepte youre howslynge suche dayly defaultes neglygē ce ye ar syker ar dedly ¶but eny know himselfe gylty dedly synne▪ owght howsled tyl shryuen • also dyuyne seruice yf eny fele remorse dedly synne wyttyng well yt dedly synne yf may esely get hys confessoure begyn hys seruice▪ ought shryuen take hys penaunce trew shryfte mouthe wt absolucion folowyng lyghtyth moche soulle gyueth conforte hope forgyuenes profytable yf yt wel chewyd mouthe swolued stomacke▪ thys holy seruyce yf yt well chowed mynde sauerly felte harte yt fedeth soulle suffycyently therfore sayth saynt bernarde yt profyteth lytel syng say theyr seruyce occupy theyre minde ther whyle thinges ar lyke man payeth hys dette wyth false money semeth golde syluer wythout y coper bra wythin whiche contentyth lorde payeth yt rather ꝓuoketh hym dysplesaunce wylfully purpose occupyeth mynde tyme holy houres thynges takyth hede sayth syngeth yf gyue stede wylfully without nede herynge seynge otherwyse eny thynge wherby distracte fro mynde aduertence ye seruyce saith though say syngfully wordes▪ ro cap • gr • ni clement • yet payeth treuly hys dette ne pleasyth god therwyth offendyth hym synneth greuously ought penaunce therfore say seruyce agen better entendaunce doyng penaunce bothe place after▪ vnderstandyth repentaunce harte shryfte wyth fulfyllynge suche penaunce hys goostly father enioyneth hym yt standyth hys dyscrescyō enioyne hym penaunce hys neglygence therwyth enioyne hym say seruyce agen thynge stede therof bothe case lyke folowe hym semeth moste spedefull hys soulles heltheinno de celeb misse ca pmo nethelesse yf haue sayde seruyce agen come shryfte shal enioyned say yt agen shall haue penaūce fyrste myssayngro capitulo graui clemē ¶but dressyth hys harte god begynnyng hys seruyce wt wyll purpose kepe mynde stable thervpō though yt happen hym afterwarde neglygence fraylte dystracte hys thoughtes sayeth besyde hys fyrste purpose yf abyde wylfully suche thoughtes hath perceyued turnyth hys mynde ye shall vnderstande yt foure thinges cause moche soche vnstablenes harte goddes seruyce ¶the firste besynes occupaciō bodely worldely vayne thyngesde sūmo bono libro tercio capitulo vii isodore medytacyon redynge gather stable hys myndes gyther make hym redy wyse man byddeth sayethecclesi xviii ante orationem prepara animam tuam y prayer make redy thy soulle shulde harpe make mynstralsy ye neglygence kepyng harte tyme seruice whiche roted lōge yuel custome frayle wretched soulle boūde borne doune yt yt sturre vp yt selfe frō wandryng vagant thoughtes yt accustomyd man rennyth downewarde frō hye hyl▪ may stynte hymselfe one goynge tyll comethe vale ryght haue vsed theyre harte renne downewarde yt wyll vpon erthly vayne thynges▪ lyghtly stynte yt ne gather yt stablenessup ioh trac xlix yuel custome saynt austyn sayth byndeth man burden beryth hym downe ¶and vagacion caused dulnes heuynes harte else slouthe whiche dullarde lyste laboure aboute kepynge hys owne harte tyl fallen suche yuel custome lyghtly breke away therfro▪ therfore remedy agenste muste sharpenes drede quycknes hope soulle dysposed ¶for lyght harted vayne condicyons nedeth case vse mynde bysely thoughtes drede hys deth hys dome paynes beholdynge therwyth pareyl stondyth yf cōtynew rechelesly suche wandryng mynde vnto deth whiche shall come woteth sone ¶thys dredful beholdynge often depely vsed contynewed may shorte time grace make hym restrayne gather gyther flowing thoughtes vanytyes ar disposed greate heuynes dulues nede thys case sharpe hymselfe drede also beholde grete goodnes charite oure mercyful lorde presence hym hys holy aungels tyme hys seruyce quycken vp theyr heuynes lerne delyte oure lorde stable mynde hym prophete saythe delectare dn̄o et dabit tibi petitiones cordis tui psal xxxvi delyte lorde shall gyue thyne harte wyll aske desyre felyth delyte him▪ desyreth nothing hym whome may haue hym nedeth ¶the thyrde thynge causeth dystraccyon prayer goddes seruyce y malyce fende y moste besy lette gyue deuoute prayer praysynge god yt brennyth hym woūdeth hym sore▪ though suffer soulle haue sōe peace eny tymes▪ non seyth yt turne prayer go goddes effectuall spedeful prayer yf yt done yt oughte▪ felly bysely laboureth malycyous enemy lette yt ¶remedy agenste y make vpon brest pryuely contyneually suche tymes token crosse wyth stronge stedfaste faythe paciently perceuerantly laboure kepe holde mynde vpon lorde vpon ye saye synge ye shall fele shall fle way yf smytten wt staffe saynt iames saythiacobi iiii resistite diabolo et fugiet vobis wtstande fende shall fle away frō eny geue stede sturrynges begynnyng play wt suche vagante thoughtes laboureth put hys mynde▪ wyl take holde brydel hym hys yuel maner lede harte moche lewdenes hym lyst therfore beware inwardely ware dryue hym way tymes ¶of vayne troubelous tyme goddes seruyce lette bothe hymselfe capi xvii thys malycyous serpent seeth thus chased many dryuē way seketh entre agayne way thē assayeth gette holde one whome sturrethe anone make vayne chere synge token wherby one tyme many ar meued maner dyssolucyon dystracte sadnes inwarde deuocyō sturreth make somwey warde token thynge comberously thrughe ar taryed theyre myndes troubeled theyre spyrytes ar dryuen quyetnes deuocyon anguysshe paynefull grudginges haste thē faster theyre armure begynne gyue batayle suche vayne troubelous sturrynges laboure gather holde theyr mynde gyther sayde before▪ else subtyll enemy wyll enter vpon theym ageyne ¶and therfore suche vayne comberous people ar fourthe cause make chyldren father fende ye wyll desyres youre father ¶if kynge meate hys seruantes aboute hym serue hym yf feylde fyghte hys knyghtes hym warre hym yf laboures hys vyne yerde hys gardyn came one made hys seruantes knyghtes hys laboures skatered flye seruice shulde suche one called traytor kynge put dothe▪ moche parlously ar traytours god vanyte trouble cause dystraccyon hys holy seruyce make myndes trew knyghtes laboures skatered ¶these ar bad felowes let comon profyt theyre felyshyp lyke vnto thornes bryers wyll suffer ye corne groweth amongest brynge forthe fruyte non yt wolde growe vp thentendaunce shulde aboute songe▪ oughte entende thys ende therafter demed ye oughte syngynge seke pleasaunce voyce ne delyte swetnes selfe songe ne hygh songe ne curyous syngyng ne maner vanyte seke cōpuncy youre synnes deuocyō god hys holy mother whose praysyng ye syngein regula ca xxxviii et capitulo xlvii ¶and though yt saynt benet sayth suche ought rede synge may edyfye herers▪ yet yt expedyente haue eny respecte harte towarde herers sōge songe moste deuoutly towarde god▪ edyfyeth moste tho ye thinke right noughte lesse ye thinke fleynge vanyte ye edyfye ¶ y necessary take hede syngynge note songe ar youre bokes eche theyre owne towne mesure syngynge euenly sette kepte oughte rewlyd spyrytes kepte reste deuocyō god furthered therby letted therfore eche one oughte haue ere yf eny dyscorde hapen▪ eche one redy gyue stede one haste fourth warde drawe backeward ought synge gyther accorde gyther ye oughte one harte ye prayse god yt wyth one voyce ¶how thys sōge thys holy seruyce oughte meke sad without vanyte curyosyte capitulo xxii y neyther syngynge ne redynge may please god selfe dysposycyon reder synger therafter yt plesyth dysplesyth oure lorde taketh hede harte thentente outwarde voyce therfore reioyse vayne glory delyte swetnes plesaunce theyr owne voyce please god wyth theyr syngynge offende hym please fende saynt gregory sayth pleasaunte voyces soughte▪ sober lyfe y forsaken ¶and therfore fende hathe grete entre vycecesarius dialog dist xii capitulo iiii somtyme vsyth yt hymselfe rede one clarke swete • ayre voyce many delyte hym synge day relygyous oughte aboute kepynge harte mekenes deuocyon yt may plese goddes syghtecesarius dialogis dist iiii capitulo viii yt writen monke abbey saynte benet abbot voyce moste pleasaunte swete thys monke halowed one paschall ester euen song swetely songe halowynge yt sowned eres herde hym yf yt melody mooste swete delycyous hymselfe suche delyte vayne glory therin▪ anon done fendes toke hym bothe soulle body sodeyne meruelous wyse man wyst ne became ¶here ye may se perylous yt y eny body delyte hym hys owne voyce outwarde songelibro x capitulo xxxiii saynte augustyne sayth hys confessyons relygyous man oure lordes dome hys hyghe vayne syngyng fende sayde thus hym songe sayde vayne glory vayne name hys voyce fel eny thinge downe waxed wery▪ lyfte yt vp hyer cam rēnynge gladly helpe elder wolde haue songe fourthe yt begonne▪ yet wyth helpe yt fauoured preuayled agenste helde fourthe hys owne gaue stede anon yt sene openly fende comynge hys mouthe lyknesse hotte brennynge yren▪ entered hys helper ¶therfore man clymbeth hygh fayleth fotynge holde somtyme fallyth breketh hys necke ryght suche hygh syngers fayle fotyng mekenes byneth haue holde deuocyon aboue falle downe pryde breke theyr neckes gostly lyke euery note meke deuoute songe shal haue specyall rewarde god▪ ryghte fende marketh euery note suche prowde sōge haue ye syngers punysshed therforeide dis quar • capitulo ix ¶for tyme clarkes sange quier wyth hygh lowde voyce relygyous man sawe fende satte hyghe wyth grete sacke hys lyfte hande ryght hande put therin theyr voyces songe seruyce done made greate ioye gladnes amonge yf praysed god wyth theyr songe ryghte well holy man sayde ye haue songe faste sayde ye haue fylled grete sacke ful asked mente tolde sene ashamed moche reioysed ¶and therfore oure saynge deuyne serui take hede entente ye say yt thentente gyueth euery good dede hys ryght name yf entente good dede good yf thentente yuel dede y yuel yuel dede may neuer made good thente neuer good thoughe yt maye lesse yuel yt y done good entente ¶but saye synge dyuyne seruice y good holy dede yt selfe▪ therfore yf yt well done good entente y good ¶therfore ye nede take hede nether ye synge ne saye thys holy seruyce vayne glory done wyll taken holy deuoute ne vayne pleasaunce seke plese thereby desyre beholde louers goddes seruyce ne vayne drede wolde come saue drede leste shulde shent ne vayne shame doo come thydre ar shamed yf ye oughte yt god good entent though creature shulde ne se eche selfe alone▪ yet ye wolde neuer lesse dylygent deuoute synge yt say yt come therto ¶and moche god asketh man y conteyned vnder one conclusyon charyte standeth loue god oure selfe oure euen chrysten oure selfe▪ therfore yt nedefull goddes seruyce ye ye entende oure lordes worshyp helthe profyt apperyth euen ¶now yt man y frayle vnstable hymselfe thynge plesyth one tyme yt dysplesyth hym nother tyme wyll wyll yt sone reasō desyreth sensualyte agayne fayth soule wolde haue flesshe contraryeth sythe one man y thus contraryous dyuerse hymselfe meruayle thoughe many men gatheryd togyther often tymes dyuerse cōtrary felynges cō dyciōs wherof riseth amongest somtyme trouble grudgeynges harte worde chere dede ¶but though yt oure power • • ape alwayes sōtyme take occasiō wherby ar • ed ageynste sōtyme thynges take occasyon meued ageynste vs▪ yet yt power grace cōsente wylfully suche sturrynges ire vnpacyence namely besy hasty put remedy ageynst redy forgyue eny thinge y done ageynste v sone aske forgyuenes fele eny y hurte v therfore saynte austyne byddeth hys rewlecapitulo vi shulde haue stryues else shulde sone ende meane thoughe moued fraylete harte eny vnpacyence shulde notte geue suche stede therto breke oute wt wordes stryfe yf ouersene breke oute stryffe muste haste v make ende thereof redy forgyfyng askynge forgyfnesse lenger suche forgyfynge askynge forgyfnesse taryed▪ lenger endureth harte sturryng ire lenger endure encrese tyl sowleys ouercome grace withdrawyth fende enteryth therfore sayeth saynte pauleephesi iiii sol non occidat super iracundiam vestram et nolite locum dare diabolo y saye suffer wrathe abyde tylle sonne goynge downe wylleth geue place fende kepyth wrathe harte▪ y occupyed wyth yuell bytter thoughtes whereby fende catchyth holde brynge hym worsecapitulo xiii ¶therfore saynte benet ordeyned hys rewle eche day ende mattyns begynnynge daye laste ende euensonge begynnynge nyghte▪ pryoure name shulde saye lowde pater noster myghte yt saynge petycyon sayeth et dimitte nobis y gyue v oure trespaces forgyue trespace v shulde sturred drawen forgyue eche othercapitulo iiii ¶for cause hathe lorde ordeyned holy rewle ye shulde euery day bynnyng euensōge eche forgyue aske forgyuenes saynge lowde harte tongue indulgete nobis forgyue v god hys moste mercyfull mother mary▪ yf haue offended wt worde dede sygne token yf eny trespace agenste vs▪ wyth moste full wylle harte forgyue yt ¶and thys ye say aue maria • oure lady therby ye shulde strōge breke downe cōtrarious sturrynges ye may forgyue veryly harte lyke ye say mouthe ¶and thys ye saye euensonge rather eny youre howres cause euensonge begynnynge nyghte said therfore sonne shulde go downe vpon youre wrathe pareyles haue rehersed before▪ ye forgyue aske forgyuenes tyme occasyons trespaces hathe hapned day ye may clene pesyble cōscience praygod wt youre euensonge holy seruyce oughte sayde wyth clene restefull harte ¶if eny ouercome wyth temptacyon ire whyche god forfende wolde say thys indulgete cause wolde forgyue▪ gretly blame yet neuer ye excused yt sayd name therfore byndethe whether saye yt saye yt whether thense therfore absente saye theyre euensonge alone oughte neuer lesse say yt thoughe none presente speke yet speke name al vnyte congregacyon forgyuenesse asked offered ye may wytte eche person sayeth forgyue eche one spake onely owne name shulde saye forgyue forgyue also yf yt sayd vnyte all▪ stande tone syde shulde forgyue eche speke gyther ouer tother syde themselfe yt shulde seme eche one sayeth yt name vnyte all▪ therfore yt byndeth forgyue pardoneth theyr trespace therfore wretched persone eny way wardenes harte wolde vnreconcyled dysceuered holy vnyte tyme ¶thys y dayely sacryfyce ye offer euery daye god euensonge tyme fygured contyne wall sacrifyce god bad moyses shulde offered dayly hym euen songe tymeexodi xxix sone goynge downe sayd wolde dwelle amongest theyr lorde god shulde well know theyr lorde god ¶therfore sewre may ye ye shall haue oure lorde god ye wylle aske hym youre helthe yf ye gette hym dwelle thus amongest dayly offerynge thys sacryfyce charyte vnyte ¶but nowe perauenture ye myghte aske whether thys askynge forgyuenesse thys indulgete suffycient eny trespace offence eny dothe agenste nother without eny specyal askeynge ¶to thys answere persone agenste whome trespace offence done▪ oughte indulgete saide quier whether bere wylfully eny heuines harte make shew eny heuynes worde dede agenste persone yt hathe offended far offēce lōgeth owne selfe owne cause though ye aske neuer forgyuenesse ne trespaces yt ar done agenste god agenst relygyō ▪ oughte correcte rewles relygyon tyme y netheles indulgete ware none kepe wrathe ne make quarell owne cause vnder coloure relygyon zele obseruaunces therof personal cause far hurte relygyon ar forgyuen indulgete y sayde thys ye may se wordes ye say eny trespace ageynste v wyth moste full wyll forgyue yt therfore eny forgyue wyll harte wordes ar sayd▪ makyth gabbynge thoughe say wordes herselfe ne sayd ar sayde quyer name bynde sayde ¶but parsone hathe wyttyngly offended nother▪ oughte y reconcyled aske forgyuenesse knoweth hathe offended▪ indulgete begynne yf wyl thoughe forgyue yt indulgete oughte speke therof▪ yet muste aske forgyuenesse afterwarde ye souerayne serches haue cure relygyon oughte se sadly correcte onely trespace yt dyd agenste syster moche obstynasy obedyence agenste intente rewle wolde seke recōcyled breketh vnyte congregacyon myghte cause oure lorde wythdrawe hys gracious presence loueth dwelle vnyte restful soulles also geueth way enmy take power ouer selfe dysceuereth herselfe vnyte holy congregacyon shepe wandereth alone vnyte flocke y sone taken deuoured wolfe ye y sayde wyll forgyue namely tyme indulgete ¶and therfore eche one oughte full ware yt kepe ne bere grudgeynge ne wrate harte though eny man hyde yt tyme warde shewynge god knoweth yt well ynoughe wythdrawyth hys grace fende catchyth holde sowle ¶now happes somme myghte thynke shall wolde fayne forgyue loke yt ye saye wythout feynynge ye wolde forgyue veryly harte ye forgyue thoughe ye fele neuer many contrary sturynges ye folowe ye sturynges worde ne dede veryly dyspleased lothe compelle youre selfe contrary suche frowarde sturynges hurte ye sowle haue oure wylle free oure felynges therfore may wylle wylle v lyste maye fele ne vnfele v lyste therfore oure mercyfull lorde takyth v oure felynges oure wylles ¶netheles though persone felte many bytter sturrynges ire vnpacyence yf dysplesaūce ther arose ageynste wyth myghty feruente wylle prayed oure lorde hys holy mother helpe wente chyrche sayde aue maria indulgete wyth couente hope gette grace ouercome hymselfe▪ trowe prayer oure lady obedyence rewle knyttynge hymselfe vnyte congregacyō ▪ shulde fele fersenesse hys sturrynges sone abated ¶thus therfore recōcyled gither ye begynne youre euensonge ye say fyue psalmes haue forgyuenesse ye haue offended god youre fyue wyttes meryte lordes fyue woundes whyche hys holy body bothe euensonge tyme day losed taken downe frome crosse euensonge tyme worlde fro begynnynge laste age worlde suffered hys holy passyon ¶antempne beati metuentes blessed ar drede lorde kepe cōmaundementes vyrgyns sōne sytteth father ryghte syde shall say come ye blyssed father receyue kyngdome y prepared begynnynge worlde ¶the chapyter beata e maria blyssed art thow marye haste borne lorde maker worlde thow haste broughte fourthe hym made endelesly thow abyddest vyrgyn ¶the hympne lux deus indeficiens hympne ar fyue verse answering nōbre fyue psalmes youre hympnes euensong foure storyes tother thre storyes ar mo fewer verse hympnes euensonge▪ thoo hympnes ar taken seruice chyrche specyally made euensōges tother foure ar ¶what hympnes psalmes antempnes betoken haue wryten mattyns ¶in tow firste verse hympne ye pray oure lorde iesu cryste gostly lyghte wythdrawyng bodely lyghte goynge downe maternall sō ne▪ lyghten oure sowlles lyghte grace sōne y gone sterres appere mynysshe darkenes nyghte▪ therfore thyrde verse ye calle oure lady sterre broughte fourthe sōne lorde iesu cryste prayng dryue darkenesse synne fourthe verse ye pray kepe youre harte wylles god▪ whyle bodyes ar aslepe fyfte verse ye praye correcte youre thoughtes wordes dedes therfore yt well done eche nyghte ye proclaymed youre selfe preuyly defaultes ye done thoughte sayde daye myghte helpe corrected clensed therof mater thys hympne ye may se euensonge longeth begynnynge nyghte sayde lux deus god art lyghte neuer saylyng lyghten thow mercyfully howse oure harte whyle beame sonne goeth waye qui virginem thow shonest aboue heuens dwellynge vyrgyn▪ nowe dwellynge heuen lyghten v lowe bynethe stella starre broughtest fourthe sonne chase awaye darkenesses dethe whiche envyous ennemye wonte brynge wandrynge sowles vt sopitis whyle bodyes sleape harte mote cleue vnto god wylle mote alway abyde redy wylle oure lorde correctrix thow correcter thoughtes wordes dedes helpe mote pleasynge thy • ōne maria mater gloria tibi v pax multa • ¶of psalme magnificat magnificat thys y ladyes songeluce primo yt y sayde euery daye eueusonge rather howres dyuerse cause ¶one euensō ge tyme worlde lady synguler assente broughte helthe mankynde ¶a nother cause y shulde dayely haue mynde incarnaciō lorde iesu cryste wroughte euentyde worlde ioye whiche thys songe made ¶the thyrde cause y oure lady lykened euen starre begynneth appere euentyde ¶the forthe cause y myndes haue bene laboured weryed day wyth many thoughtes besynesses shulde cōforted wyth songe ioye oure lady holpen prayer ageynste temptacyons nyghteluce primo ¶the gospell sheweth onre lady conceyued oure lorde iesu cryste cytye nazareth▪ none wente ierusalem cosyn elyzabeth mother saynte iohn̄ baptyste comynge thyder saynte iohn̄ ioyed hys mother wombe hys mother fylled spyryte prophesy blyssed oure lady sayde blyssed thow amongest woman blyssed fruyte thy wombe oure lady tellyth saynte birgyttelibro sexto capitulo lix sturred harte wyth vnspecable vnknowen gladnesse moche sowle mighte skante holde yt selfe ioye holy tongue brake oute wt wordes praysynge god wythoute studye thynkeynge sayde magnificat anima mea dominū sowle prayseth lorde et exultauit spyryte hathe ioyed god sauyoure ¶here may lerne oure lady forsake veyne ioye aūgell bene heuen cōceyued sōne god elyzabeth blyssed praysed worthy mother god al thys meued vanyte ne presumpcion selfe mekenesse praysynge ioyeng god faynedly tongue inwardenesse sowle therfore sayeth mouthe sowle prayseth sowle ioyeth selfe god y maker thynges y become man sauyoure mankynde oure lady therfore y specyally syngulerly none others wyse helthe saluacion y come man therfore sayeth spyryte y sowlle hathe ioyed god sauyoure sayeth saynt bede spyryte ioyeth god hys sauyoure▪ delyteth nothynge y erthe ne y plesyd plente goodes worshyppes ne y broken wyth grudgeynge vnpacyence eny trybulacyon dysease▪ onely delyteth ioyeth mynde hys maker whome hopeth haue endelesse helthe quia respexit hathe beholde mekenesse hys hande mayden oure lady tellyth praysed ioyed god god become syngulerly behelde mekenesse wherby ye may se mekenesse cause god chase hys mother therfore sayeth saynte ierome y noble worthy mother god▪ y bryghte worshypfulle whome bryghtenesse father glory chase hymselfe▪ y chaste▪ bare body body cryste▪ yet sayeth god behelde onely mekenesse y keper vertewes fel therof▪ ecce enim ec hoc beatam dicent omnes generationes lo hense •• che generacyons shall calle blyssed ¶all generacions heuen erthe crysten hethen iewes sarazyns men woman poure ryche men aungels ryght wyse synners wedded syngle soueraynes subiectes shal say blyssed shal prayse blyssednesse god sauyoure hathe wroughte wyth hathe gyuen euery nacyon people turned faythe cryste▪ prayse worshyppe hys holy mother quia fecit y myghty hathe done greate thynges hys name y holy greate thynges made kepte clene synne halowed endowed wyth gyftes holy goste toke body creature broughte furthe maker hys seruaunte bare lorde vyrgyn y mother god boughte mankynde broughte hys chosen endelesse lyfe greate thynges dyd y myghty rewarde aboue eny man maye deserue y myghty hathe done myghty greate thynges hys name y holy y good holy may thoughte spoken hys holy name mannes meryte hathe done greate thynges helthe man et misericordia eius hys mercy y kynred kynredes drede hym thys y mercy hathe wroughte oure lady hys incarnacyō passyon mankynde mercy saluacion dauid asked sayde ostende nobis domine misericordiam tuam psalmo 84 lorde shew v thy mercy yf sayde thow haste shewed v thy power makynge thynges noughte thow haste shewed v thy wysdome meruaylous gouernynge thynges thow haste shewed v thy ryghtwysnes punysshynge synne bothe aungel men therfore shew v thy mercy incarnacyon thy sonne saluacyon manne thys mercy bryngeth oure lady furthe sayeth hys mercy y kynred kynredes one kynred kynreddes kynred iewes kynreddes worlde amongeste iewes thys mercy wroughte warde spred abrode vnto people take profyte saluacyon thys mercy thoughe yt suffycyent men nedeth yet yt auayleth dyspose therto y dysposycyon▪ drede god wythoute drede none maye saued drede payne drede god oure lady sayeth timentibus eum hys mercy y drede hym fecit potenciam brachio suo hathe done powre arme y saye hys sonne arme cometh body hande bothe arme body▪ sonne hathe hys beyng father holy gooste bothe father sonne thys arme y hys sonne hathe done power hym made thynges hym saued mankynde hym hathe throwen downe power fendes therfore sayeth oure lady dis persit superbos mente cordis sui hathe dysparsed prowde wylle thy harte ¶these prowde fendes iewes prowde people hooste y dysparsed y myghty fyghte ryghte prowde fendes dysparsed passyon oure lorde iesu cryste myghty warre agenste man ¶the prowde iewes also wolde meke faythe iesu cryste ar dysparsed abrode worlde moche haue nether londe ne contre ne cyte ne towne theyre owne dwelle erthe somme dwelle one londe somme nother somme one cytye somme nother vnder trybute thraldome chrysten people thus fendes iewes dysparsed oure lorde wylle hys harte y say ryghtefulle iudgemente hys preuy dome ¶all prowde people also dysparsed mynde theyre owne hartrs meke people lyue vnyte reste ryghte prowde people bothe scattered theyre owne harte many vanytyes vnlefull desyres also deuyded agenste trouble enuye debate deposuit potentes de sede hathe putte downe myghty frome seate hathe lyfte vp meke ¶these myghty haue greate power temporall spyrytuall mysse vse yt agenste wylle god ageynste theyre euen chrysten ageynste theyr owne sowlles helthe myghty god throwyth downe seate grace grace god shulde haue hys seate theyre harte frome seate dygnyte power whyche mysse vse sete cōnynge wysdome ar blynded theyre owne malyce laste sete dome wylfull powre shall sytte deme wyth crystemath xix shall demed ende worlde seate shall suche myghty throwen downe sete shall meke lyfted vp hathe lyfte vp meke grace blysse euerlastynge wordes oure lady spake prophesy thynge come yet sayeth yf yt paste syckernesse fulfyllynge yt sycker fulfylled tyme come yf yt bene past cause prophetes vsed ofte suche maner spekynge esurientes impleuit bonis hathe fylled hongry wyth goodes▪ ryche hathe lefte voyde ¶bodely hongre appetyte meate gostely honger desyre grace vertues hongry hathe nede meate hongry gostly thynketh hathe noughte good y namely hymselfe ne hys owne merytes feleth hymselfe nedy goodes▪ therfore seketh desyreth laboureth faste gette suche hongry▪ god fylleth wyth goodes spirituall grace endelesse blysse ¶but ryche ar presume themselfe wene better haue haue tokonne canne haue canne may coūte yt theyre owne merytes worthynesse though yt came themselfe ryche god leuyth voyde grace glory ar wylfully poure frō worldely welthes comfortes honger desyre goddes grace heuenly comfortes▪ theyre desyre shall fulfylled haue rychesse worldely prosperyte take theyr ioye comforte therin seke none other▪ shall lefte voyde goodes temporall euerlastynge suscepit israel hathe taken israel chylde hathe mynde hys mercy ¶israel one patriarkes called also iacob whose lynage oure lady came therfore oure lady sayeth ye god hathe taken israel yt y say body mankynde ye lynage israel whyche israel y called goddes chylde meke obedyente god chylde father thys dede god hathe mynde hys mercy whiche promysed patriarkes prophetes wolde become mangenesis xxii therfore sayeth oure lady sicut locutus est hathe sayde oure father y patriarkes prophetes begynnynge worlde specyally abraham hys sede y people come abraham bodely generacyon whome oure lady came oure lorde iesu cryste onely helpe people trewly folowe faythe leuynge abraham vnto ende worlde properly called sede chyldren abraham whome shulde parteners fruyte oure lordes comynge endelesly ioye blysse amen ¶antempne patrem cum filio oure sowlles ioyenge mote contynewally prayse father wyth sonne holy goste wyth eyther one god whiche endelesly knowynge oure fraylte endelesly ordeyned vyrgyn mary oure helper whose sowlle ioynge god praysed hym soueraynely antempne rosa rorans byrgytte arte vessell grace rose dewynge goodnesse sterre droppynge clerenesse dew thou pytye heuen droppe clennesse lyfe vale wretchednesse antempne birgitta byrgytte droppe myrre exāpler abstynence thow haste made playster penaūce sorowfull peple whyle thow wrote wordes cryste thow arte new lyghte chyrche defēder norysher meke meyne thy howsolde ¶myrre y bytter gomme taste smell yt swete yt kepyth deade bodyes rottynge therfore yt betokeneth penaūce bytter felynge sorowe sharpenes yt smellyth swete goddes syghte yt helpyth sowlle dede synne kepyth yt endeles corrupcyon suche droppe myrre saynte byrgytte bothe example owne lyueynge warnynge gaue people mystyef shulde falle synne amended mercy grace myghte haue yf wolde turne amende▪ made holsome playster penaunce people y sorowfully combred synnes worde cryste wrote reuelacyons heuen enformacyon mankynde therfore called new lyghte gyuen holy chyrche thys laste worlde mayne tho serue haue deuocyon specyally professed relygyon ¶oratio deus qui ecclesiam mercyfull god haste vouched safe lyghten thy chyrche blyssed byrgytte wyth holy counsayle examples▪ graunte prayer mote fullfylle dede wyth deuoute sowlles tho thynges thow haste mercyfully shewed reuelacyon clensynge oure synnes per dominū nostrum ¶of complyn collacyon complyn y seuenthe laste howre dyuyne seruyce yt y moche say fulfyllynge ende therof seuen howres dyuyne seruyce ar fulfylled therewyth also ended fulfylled spekynge etynge drynkynge laborynge bodely besynesses tyme oughte kepte grete stylnes strayth scylence onely wordes also noyses dedes saue preuy softe prayer holy thynkeynge bodely sleape complyn betokeneth ende mannes lyfe ende worlde chosen oure lorde shall delyuered trauayle wo broughte endelesse quiete reste therefore eche persone oughte dyspose hym bedde warde yf hys bedde hys graue man dyeth borne hys graue buryed righte complyn tyme ye shulde dysposed yf ye dyynge kepe sober stylle afterwarde yf ye deade fro bodely dedes wordes token therof responce complyn ye praye lady cōmende handes kepynge sōne man dyenge sayeth manus tuas cōmendeth hys sowlle god dyuerse thynges ye saye complyn accordeth ¶and ende also complyn ye haue collacion y redde spyrytuall matter gostly edyfycacion helpe gather gyther scaterynges mynde outewarde thynges therfore maner bokes oughte redde tyme • onely tho bokes ar inwardely spyrytuall easy vnderstande sowlles maye fedde therwyth holpen thereby kepe themselfe inwarde peace stablenesse mynde nyghte folowynge onely tongue oughte kepte nyghtes tyme deade speche bodyes dedes▪ also harte oughte fulle besyly kepte vagaunte thoughtes bothe tylle ye falle slepe ye wake eny tyme nyghte anon ye wake aryse holy father cassianus sayeth thinges yt necessary v haue waker besy kepynge oure selfe nyghtes tyme clene besy kepynge harte outwarde wyttes day maketh redy body sowlle kepe clennes chastyte nyghte ryghte waker stable kepynge harte deuoute holy thoughtes prayer nyghte watche arrayeth gyueth grete inwarde strengthe sadnesse sowlle obseruaūces dedes done day ¶thus ye may se many holy obseruaunces ioyned youre dyuyne seruyce cause alwayes take hede haue mynde vpon youre helthe begynnynge eche howre ye saye pater noster aue sturre vp youre deuocion hys seruice ende eche howre ye synge aue maria wyth collecte folowyng kepe deuocyon ye haue gathered therin tyerce ye begynne speke ye go graue arme name blessed trinyte mynde youre dethe youre dome ageynst temptacyons youre dayly dedes euensonge ye aske graunte forgyuenesse eche wyth indulgete complyn ye arraye wyth deuoute herynge holy doctryne youre collacion ¶and yt deuociō ye go youre complyn whiche hathe verse begynnynne y sayde howres y conuerte no god oure sauyoure conuerte v turne v et auerte turne away thy wrathe v rede many tymes folke haue fallen mystyef nyghtes tyme theyr sinnes thefore euen begynnynge complyn holy chyrche prayeth chyldren may conuerted synne oure lorde turne hys wrathe also howres dyuyne seruyce oughte drede haue offended god sōme neglygence y none dothe welle thynke hymselfe dothe welle dredyth defaute dede▪ maye thoughte sykernesse make hymselfe gylty seyth defaute hymselfe oughte drede l •• te blynde blyndenesse may worse hym many greatesynnes sene sorowed therfore yeldynge v gylty god daye▪ aske euen cōuerted amendemente pray lorde kepe hys ire v say begynnynge complyn conuerte no ¶the comoun vse chyrche say foure psalmes complyn saynte benet settyth hys rewle thre psalmes sayde complyn therto accordeth youre seruice hathe complyn thre psalmes whiche memento domine ecce qm bonū ecce nunc fyrste psalme memento ye behyghte ye wyll nether go bedde ne slepe tyl ye haue foūde selfe restynge place lorde god shall tother tow psalmes teche tone y ecce qm bonum tellyth loue vnyte eche one oughte haue wt tother y ecce nunc spekyth praysynge ioye oughte oure lorde god sowlle euer tow thynges y vnyte peace loue ioye god▪ therelyketh oure lorde reste abyde therfore yf ye say well youre complyn ye shall wythoute tow yf ye fele tow veryly▪ blysse go bedde slepe restfully safely oure lorde hymselfe restyth wyll kepe whyle ye slepe ¶antempne iocundum est y mery dwel one▪ yt inderest harte bysely worshyp god moder ¶the chapyter multe filie many doughters haue gathered richesse thow alone mooste holy mary haste ouer paste many doughters chosen sowlles whiche haue gathered rychesse meny grace vertewes lady passyth all▪ alone grace vertues parfytly al saintes ¶responce manus tui noble gloryous vyrgyn cōmende v handes power thy sonne uerse quem redemptorem whome knowlege ageynebyer god trouthe ¶a nother responce manus tuas • betake sowlle lorde thy handes uerse redemisti thow haste boughte ageyne lorde god trouthe ¶the hympne ¶ingenitore ye fyrste verse hympne ye knowlege faythe blyssed trinite ¶and seconde verse ye saye blessed trinyte bothe heuen maydens wombe thre persones become man euer sonne y father holy gooste ¶in thyrde verse ye saye tho thre persones y one godhed onely oure lady y maydenhed motherhed ¶in fourthe verse ye knowlege sonne y god man none saue hathe vyrgyn hys moder ¶in fyfte verse ye pray god beholde hys mercyes forsake ¶then ye begyn say thus genitore sonne y father father sonne holy goste eyther eyther y holy goste hii marie thre per parsones dwellynge maydenly bowelles marye kepte hye peace thy worde ¶thys man glad dye peace mankynde come whome shulde broughte endelesse peace tyme went helle wyste delyueryd thys man seker hys delyueraunce hys sauyoure hys armes therfore ioyfully sayde lorde thow lettest thy seruaunte dye peace thy worde thow behyghtest quia viderunt myne eyne haue sene thy sauyoure ye chylde bare hys armes whiche y sauyoure hys trew people hym se wt hys bodely eyne hys manhod hym se hys gostely eyne faythe hys godhed quod parasti whome yu haste made redy face people ¶he y mannes face may esely sene faythe knowlege sauyoure iesu cryste made open apostle people therfore laste doume shall sene manhod mercyfulle sauyoure faythe drede loue beholde hym theyre face turne theyr backe hym mysbyleue deadely synne dye▪ shall sene moste ferefulle iudge thus thys holy man sayth y made redy face peple iewes also hethen therfohe sayeth farther lumen ad reuelacionem thow haste made lyghte lyghtenynge hethen people glory thy people israel ¶the hethen shulde parteners ioy sōme tho aungels dispysed hym felle mystyef abode praysyng god knowyng falle theyr felowes shulde reparelyd oure lady ¶there precyous stone called carboncle whyche shyneth bryghte fyre hys owne kynde darkenesse may blemysshe yt ne moysture quenche yt thys stone ye lyken oure lorde god ye saye per se lucens carboncle shynynge yt selfe nedeth none lyghte god alone endelesly suffycyente hymselfe claro creauir made bryghte aungels hys owne goodn̄esse wyllynge shulde made parteners hys glory exercitus anon hoste aungels se selfe made • sōme waxte prowde dyspyfed hys mother ¶antempne filu hominum sonnes men brynge ye glory worshyp vyrgyns sonne ye may made sonnes god antiphona conuerte domina lady mother ioye turne oure sorowe ioye close v aboute ioye ioyenge mote shew trouye god uerse angelorum moste myghty lady aungels responce esto nobis v defender gyle wycked benedictio ad cietatem quene aungels mote lede v felyshyp hyghe cytezyns amen fyrste lesson sciens ita que deus lessō tellyth god charite made greate multytude aungels▪ sōme felle dampnacyō sōme bode blysse abode blysse knowlege oure ladye vnmade shulde moste nere god aboue al therfore ioy thē theyr owne makynge therfore aungel sayeth thus sciens ita que deus god knowynge thynge suffycyente hīselfe endelesly hymselfe hys owne ioye moued feruoure charite • e sōme thinge myght parteners vnspecable ioye creauit • gnur therfor made vnspecable multytude aūgels geuynge free choyse theyr power▪ wolde • lyke constrayned nede feruoure hys owne charyte made theyr owne endelesse delyte▪ ryghte cōpelled owne free wylle shulde gyue contynually wythout ceasynge theyr maker charyte charyte reuerence vnfaylynge comforte eodem poynte made sōme mooste wyckedly mysse vsynge moste acceptable gyfte free choyse▪ began malycyously haue enuye theyr maker whome oughte hys moste loue soueraynely haue loued vnde protinus wherfore felle anon wyth theyr malyse deserued▪ fro euerlastynge felycyte endelesse wretchednesse alii vero aungels abode theyr charyte blysse prepared whyche loued god feruently loue beholdynge hym fayrenesse power verteu intellexerunt aungels also vnderstode syghte contemplacyon god onely wythoute begynnynge without endynge themselfe made hym hys goodnesse power goodnesse euer nouerunt knew also gloryous syghte hym selfe made wyse wysdome▪ yt se clerely demenyng goddes sufferaūce al thynges come whych toke moste inwarde affeccyon▪ knew god wolde hys charyte mekenesse hys glory comforte hys hoste y saye aungels fulfylle agayne tho heuenly mansyons whyche inobedyente aungels wretchedly felle theyre pryde enuye intuebantur se also blessyd myroure y god theyr maker certayne reuerente seate nye god hymselfe yt semed vnpossyble eny seate nyghe vnto hym knew well ye thinge yet vnmade whome sete prepared withoute begynnynge ex intuitu also charyte god wythoute doubte enfla • med poynte momente instante beholdynge clerenesse god eche loued hymselfe nethelesse loued god moste aboue thynges loued thynge vnmade shu • de sette seate nexte vnto god▪ themselfe se god loued souereynly thynge vnmade moste ioye therof omnium consolatio vyrgyn mary comforte thow art thynge whome aungels begynnynge theyr makynge brente grete charyte▪ thoughe ioyed maye spoken swetnesse clerenesse nyghe syghte god▪ yet ioyed moche thou shuldest nerer god knew reserued charyte swetnesse hadde videbant se also vpon seate certayne crowne greate fayrenesse greate worthynesse▪ maieste none safe god alone shulde ouer passe yt vnde qmuis wherfore thoughe knew god shulde veryly haue greate worshyp ioye made them▪ yet se worshyppe ioy shulde come god thow shuldest made hygh crowne et ideo ipsi therfore aungels ioyed god wolde make the▪ god made et sic tu thou vyrgyn moste holy souerayne delyte god hymselfe withoute begynnynge ioye aungels anone made et sic vere veryly god aungels aungels wyth god ioyed moste inwardely ere thou made virgyn worthy creature tu autem ¶responce te sanctum aūgels heuen prayse holy lorde sayng lorde praysynge worshyp belongeth ¶uerse cherubyn cherubyn seraphyn order heuen erye praysynges ye lorde thy glory vyrgyn saynge te decet lorde praysynge worshyp belongeth ¶benedictio matrem vyrgyn chosen yt mother god mote shew v whiche righte way vnto heuen ¶the seconde lesson intendens igitur deus thys lesson aungel sheweth god hathe worshyp aungels ioye man profyte lady al creature euer made erthe sheweth also holy vertues workes oure lady lykened dyuerse creature god made begynnynge worlde thus begynneth intendens igitur therfore god preposynge make worlde wyth creature therein▪ sayde fiat yt made gene primo et statim anon parfytly made entended make mundo ita que worlde creature saue onely man parfytly made reuerentely presente fairenesse syghte god yet lesse worlde vnmade p̄sente god wyth fayrenesse wher shulde come glorye god myrthe aungels profyte echeman wolde vse goodnesse yt thys worlde predulcis moste swete lady vyrgyn mary amyable louely profytable all▪ full conuenyently thou arte vnderstande thys lesse worlde ex scriptura gene primo men also knoweth scrypture yt plesed god departe lyghte frō darkenesse worlde sothe departynge lyghte darkenesse shulde made thy makynge plesed hym moche y saye ignorance thy tender chyldehode whiche y lykened darckenesse shulde wyse departe knowynge god whyche y lykened lyghte wyth wylle vnderstandynge lyue hys wylle shulde abyde moste fully wt moste feruente charyte cōuenienter ita que cōuenyently tendernesse yong chyldehod lykened darckenesse whiche yonge chyldehode god y knowen ne y reason ne dyscresciō wyt y done hanc vti que thow vyrgyn clene fro synne haste ouerpassed thys tendernes yonge age gene primo moste innocently deinde furthermore god made tow lyghtes wyth starres also necessary thys worlde one day nother nyghte▪ se tow lyghtes shulde made moche bryghte primum thy fyrste lyghte thy godly obedyence whyche shone moste clerely ye sōne heuen aūgels worlde good men whome god veryly euerlastynge daye secundum secōde lyghte thy moste stable faythe whiche lyghte mone many nyghtes tyme y frome howre whyche maker thynges shulde suffer dethe hys manhod hys creature vnto resurreccyon▪ wandrynge wretchedly darkenesse dyspayre mysbyleue▪ shulde broughte agayne knowlege trouthe stellis thoughtes also thy harte apered lyke vnto starres • tyme thou haddest fyrste knowyng god thou abodest feruente charyte god vnto thy dethe▪ thy thoughtes appered brighte syghte god aungels starres syghte men volucrum also hyghe flyghtes swete sownynge songes byrdes dyuerse kyndes▪ bytokened al wordes thy lyppes whyche shulde stye wyth swetnesse frome thyne erthely bodye vnto eres hym ye settyth trone mageste souerayn ioy aūgels preterea • furthermore thow lyke erthe thynges haue erthely body worlde shulde noryshed ye fruytes erthe ryghte thynge shulde onely take noryshynge thy fruyte also selfe lyfe florigeris thy workes also myghte worthyly lykened florysshynge fruytefull tree thou shuldest greate charyte shulde delyte god hys aungels fayrenesse al flowres swetnesse al fruytes prefertim • namely whyle yt byloued wythout doute god se thy makynge mo vertues kyndes herbes flowres tree fruytes stone metalles mighte founde brede worlde vnde wherfore meruayle thoughe god delyte thow lesse worlde yet made▪ thys worlde nam licet thoughe worlde made yet yt perysshe wyth thynges therin thow thyne vnfaylynge fayrenesse endelesse fore ordenaunce god shuldest abyde vndepartably moste loued loue nullo worlde deserued nothynge ne myghte deserue shulde made euerlasting sed tu thow blyssed mary moste fulle vertues haste thy makynge moste worthyly deserued helpynge grace god wyth perfeccyon vertues▪ thinges god hathe vouchedsafe wyth tu aufem ¶respōce benedicta blessed erthe whose flowres fade whose fruyte y lyfe lyue geuyng noryshynge mankynde ¶uerse vere southe thys erthe y vyrgyn mother flowres workes sonne y fruyte ¶thus verse expouneth responce bothe accordeth lesson ye maye se ¶benediccio corona quiene arayed croune vertues▪ redy v contynewally defense amen ¶the thyrde lesson virtutum omnium thys lesson y tolde cause god gaue man aūgel fre choyse whyther wolde good yuel god y worshyped specyally wyth three crownes fyrste crowne y vertew whyche made aungels seconde crowne y verteu whyche made man thyrde crowne y verteu whyche made oure lady reparynge bothe man aūgels lesson begynneth thus virtutum omnium god y worker vertues selfe vertew yt y vnposyble creature made▪ shyne eny verteu wythoute hys helpe qui principio whyche begynnynge made worlde creatures▪ laste hys verteu made man geuynge hym fre choyse hym shulde stande parseuerantly good good rewarde falle yuell yuell rewarde nam sicut agenste men theyr workes acounted lytell wylle worke tyll compelled worke stockes fetter theyr workes ar worthy loue ryghte good rewarde constrayned free wylle haue pure charyte▪ lyke wyse yf god gyuen free choyse aungels men shulde seme maner cōpelled tho thynges shulde theyr workes worthy lytel rewarde placuit igit therfore yt plesed verteu y god hymselfe gyue fredome wolde made fully vnderstōde rewarde godly obedyence shulde deserue paynes prowde vnobediēce shulde make folowers worthy magnam grete verteu god shewed made man erthe ye ende charite mekenes shulde deserue made dweller mansyon heuen whyche aūgels cōtrary goddes wylle wretchedly cast pryde enuye erant enim vertues hateful whiche might hyly haue crowned nam nulli yt doubte none kynge honored worshyped kyngly crowne eche verteu worshypeth doer amōgest men also yt arayeth hym excellently wt ashynyng crowne god aūgels therfore eche vereteu may cōuenyently called shynyng crowne vnde wherfore nōbre crounes beleued vnthyncable wt whiche god hym selfe shyneth moste hyly whose vertues ouerpasse wt lykensse multytude gretnes worthynesse thynges yt ar shal wroughte neuer thynge vertues whome yet specially thre vtues arayed gloryously thre bryghte crownes virtu nan que vertu whiche made aūgels hys fyrst crowne whiche sōme thē hauyng enuy glory god wretchedly depryued themselfe illa quo que verteu made man hym seconde crowne whyche selfe man also sodeynly priued hys owne foly consentynge enuyful sturrer suggestoure verūptamen nethelesse verteu god glory verteu mighte made lesse falle tho aungels man thoughe selfe made vngloryous thyr wyckednes felle glory wolde gyue glory god made hys theyre owne glory mooste wyse wysdome god chaunged theyre wyckednesse glory hys verteu virtu vero verteu whyche made desyderable vyrgyn hys endeles glory▪ gloryfyed hym thyrde crowne whyche aungels knew brekynges fyrste crownes shulde made hole agayne vnde domina wherfore lady hope oure helthe thow mayste ryghtefully called crownde goddes worshyp wroughte moste souerayne verteu▪ ryghte moste souerayne worshyp came hym creature clare vti que clerely yt knowen aungels thow vnmade presente goddes syghte thow shuldest thy holy mekenesse ouercome fende whiche pryde dampned hymselfe hys malyce begyled man igitur qmuis therfore thoughe aungels se man falle greate wretchednes yet myghte sorowe ioye syghte god namely yt open inoughe thynges greate thynges god shulde vouchesafe wyth thy mekenesse thy makynge responce christi virgo moste loued vyrgyn chryst worker vertues brynge helpe wretch helpe lady •• ye contynually vnto uerse quoniam borne downe wyth burden synnes▪ pray holy uerse benedicat cheualry heuen blysse god responce pro suo vnspecable glorye hys mooste worthy mother v thow arte lordes gatt whyche ryghtfull men enter kyngedome heuen ¶the hympne deus plasmator thys hympne ye prayse god syx thynges thre thynges ye aske hym fyrst ye prayse hym god man seconde ye prayse hym largenesse hys charite whiche made man gaue hym free choyse wolde thyrde ye prayse hym hys ryghtwesnesse punysshed ryghtfully bothe man aungel mysvsed thys fredom forthe ye prayse hym bothe ryght wesnes mercy forsaketh ryghtfully harded synne mercyfully receyueth penaūce also releueth meke thēselfe bereth downe enhaūce thēselfe v ye prayse hym large hys behestes thē obaye bydynges vi ye prayse hym trew fulfyllyng ꝓmesses bothe geuyng payne ye wycked blysse ye good therfore ye aske hym iii thynges one ye redy kepe ye byddeth nother yt ye rewarded wt chosen ye thyrde though ye
